dignity (‘dhignidhi) n., pl. -ies. 1 karaamo. e.g. We should respect the dignity of our country. 2 haybad; hannaan muuqaal. e.g. He walked with great dignity. 3 qab; sharaf. e.g. It was beneath his dignity to accept food and shelter from a refugee camp. 4 jago, xil, ama mas'uuliyad; garaaddo sare.

-stand on one's dignity, qof u istaaga ama dhawra sharaftiisa.

digraph (‘dhaay,garaaf) n. laba xaraf oo lammaan looguna dhawaaqo hal ahaan, sida ph, dh, sh. -digraphic adj.
